<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>
<s> you have disgraced me gentlemen <\s>
<s> bring in the men <\s>
<s> he sits motionless staring before him <\s>
<s> the board draws hurriedly together and forms a group <\s>
<s> tench in a frightened manner speaks into the hall <\s>
<s> underwood almost forces enid from the room wilder <\s>
<s> hurriedly what's to be said to them <\s>
<s> tench writes in his book wanklin <\s>
<s> very well then i ask the chairman to put it to the board <\s>
<s> with a great sigh slowly we have been made the subject of an attack <\s>
<s> looking round at wilder and scantlebury with ironical contempt i take it on my shoulders <\s>
<s> i am seventy six years old <\s>
<s> i have been chairman of this company since its inception two and thirty years ago <\s>
<s> i have seen it pass through good and evil report <\s>
<s> my connection with it began in the year that this young man was born <\s>
<s> edgar bows his head <\s>
<s> anthony gripping his chair goes on i have had do to with men for fifty years i've always stood up to them i have never been beaten yet <\s>
<s> i have fought the men of this company four times and four times i have beaten them <\s>
<s> it has been said that i am not the man i was <\s>
<s> he looks at wilder however that may be i am man enough to stand to my guns <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger <\s>
<s> the double doors are opened <\s>
<s> enid slips in followed by underwood who restrains her the men have been treated justly they have had fair wages we have always been ready to listen to complaints <\s>
<s> it has been said that times have changed if they have i have not changed with them <\s>
<s> it has been said that masters and men are equal <\s>
<s> there can only be one master in a house <\s>
<s> where two men meet the better man will rule <\s>
<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture of dismissal shall i bring them in sir <\s>
<s> frost goes out anthony turns to face his son i come to the attack that has been made upon me <\s>
<s> edgar with a gesture of deprecation remains motionless with his head a little bowed a woman has died <\s>
<s> i am told that her blood is on my hands i am told that on my hands is the starvation and the suffering of other women and of children <\s>
<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>
<s> if i fall under his feet as fall i may i shall not complain <\s>
<s> that will be my look out and this is his <\s>
<s> i cannot separate as i would these men from their women and children <\s>
<s> a fair fight is a fair fight <\s>
<s> let them learn to think before they pick a quarrel <\s>
<s> in a low voice but is it a fair fight father <\s>
<s> look at them and look at us <\s>
<s> they've only this one weapon <\s>
<s> grimly and you're weak kneed enough to teach them how to use it <\s>
<s> it seems the fashion nowadays for men to take their enemy's side <\s>
<s> i have not learnt that art <\s>
<s> is it my fault that they quarrelled with their union too <\s>
<s> there is such a thing as mercy <\s>
<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>
<s> with suppressed passion you accuse me of injustice of what amounts to inhumanity of cruelty <\s>
<s> edgar makes a gesture of horror a general frightened movement wanklin <\s>
<s> in a grim voice these are the words of my own son <\s>
<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>

<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture of dismissal shall i bring them in sir <\s>
<s> frost goes out anthony turns to face his son i come to the attack that has been made upon me <\s>
<s> edgar with a gesture of deprecation remains motionless with his head a little bowed a woman has died <\s>
<s> i am told that her blood is on my hands i am told that on my hands is the starvation and the suffering of other women and of children <\s>
<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>
<s> if i fall under his feet as fall i may i shall not complain <\s>
<s> that will be my look out and this is his <\s>
<s> i cannot separate as i would these men from their women and children <\s>
<s> a fair fight is a fair fight <\s>
<s> let them learn to think before they pick a quarrel <\s>
<s> in a low voice but is it a fair fight father <\s>
<s> look at them and look at us <\s>
<s> they've only this one weapon <\s>
<s> grimly and you're weak kneed enough to teach them how to use it <\s>
<s> it seems the fashion nowadays for men to take their enemy's side <\s>
<s> i have not learnt that art <\s>
<s> is it my fault that they quarrelled with their union too <\s>
<s> there is such a thing as mercy <\s>
<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>
<s> with suppressed passion you accuse me of injustice of what amounts to inhumanity of cruelty <\s>
<s> edgar makes a gesture of horror a general frightened movement wanklin <\s>
<s> in a grim voice these are the words of my own son <\s>
<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>
<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>

<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>
<s> you have disgraced me gentlemen <\s>
<s> bring in the men <\s>
<s> he sits motionless staring before him <\s>
<s> the board draws hurriedly together and forms a group <\s>
<s> tench in a frightened manner speaks into the hall <\s>
<s> underwood almost forces enid from the room wilder <\s>
<s> hurriedly what's to be said to them <\s>
<s> tench writes in his book wanklin <\s>
<s> very well then i ask the chairman to put it to the board <\s>
<s> with a great sigh slowly we have been made the subject of an attack <\s>
<s> looking round at wilder and scantlebury with ironical contempt i take it on my shoulders <\s>
<s> i am seventy six years old <\s>
<s> i have been chairman of this company since its inception two and thirty years ago <\s>
<s> i have seen it pass through good and evil report <\s>
<s> my connection with it began in the year that this young man was born <\s>
<s> edgar bows his head <\s>
<s> anthony gripping his chair goes on i have had do to with men for fifty years i've always stood up to them i have never been beaten yet <\s>
<s> i have fought the men of this company four times and four times i have beaten them <\s>
<s> it has been said that i am not the man i was <\s>
<s> he looks at wilder however that may be i am man enough to stand to my guns <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger <\s>
<s> the double doors are opened <\s>
<s> enid slips in followed by underwood who restrains her the men have been treated justly they have had fair wages we have always been ready to listen to complaints <\s>
<s> it has been said that times have changed if they have i have not changed with them <\s>
<s> it has been said that masters and men are equal <\s>
<s> there can only be one master in a house <\s>
<s> where two men meet the better man will rule <\s>
<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture of dismissal shall i bring them in sir <\s>
<s> frost goes out anthony turns to face his son i come to the attack that has been made upon me <\s>
<s> edgar with a gesture of deprecation remains motionless with his head a little bowed a woman has died <\s>
<s> i am told that her blood is on my hands i am told that on my hands is the starvation and the suffering of other women and of children <\s>
<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>
<s> if i fall under his feet as fall i may i shall not complain <\s>
<s> that will be my look out and this is his <\s>
<s> i cannot separate as i would these men from their women and children <\s>
<s> a fair fight is a fair fight <\s>
<s> let them learn to think before they pick a quarrel <\s>
<s> in a low voice but is it a fair fight father <\s>
<s> look at them and look at us <\s>
<s> they've only this one weapon <\s>
<s> grimly and you're weak kneed enough to teach them how to use it <\s>
<s> it seems the fashion nowadays for men to take their enemy's side <\s>
<s> i have not learnt that art <\s>
<s> is it my fault that they quarrelled with their union too <\s>

<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>

<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture of dismissal shall i bring them in sir <\s>
<s> frost goes out anthony turns to face his son i come to the attack that has been made upon me <\s>
<s> edgar with a gesture of deprecation remains motionless with his head a little bowed a woman has died <\s>
<s> i am told that her blood is on my hands i am told that on my hands is the starvation and the suffering of other women and of children <\s>
<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>
<s> if i fall under his feet as fall i may i shall not complain <\s>
<s> that will be my look out and this is his <\s>
<s> i cannot separate as i would these men from their women and children <\s>
<s> a fair fight is a fair fight <\s>
<s> let them learn to think before they pick a quarrel <\s>
<s> in a low voice but is it a fair fight father <\s>
<s> look at them and look at us <\s>
<s> they've only this one weapon <\s>
<s> grimly and you're weak kneed enough to teach them how to use it <\s>
<s> it seems the fashion nowadays for men to take their enemy's side <\s>
<s> i have not learnt that art <\s>
<s> is it my fault that they quarrelled with their union too <\s>
<s> there is such a thing as mercy <\s>
<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>
<s> with suppressed passion you accuse me of injustice of what amounts to inhumanity of cruelty <\s>
<s> edgar makes a gesture of horror a general frightened movement wanklin <\s>
<s> in a grim voice these are the words of my own son <\s>
<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>
<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>

<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>
<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>
<s> you have disgraced me gentlemen <\s>
<s> bring in the men <\s>
<s> he sits motionless staring before him <\s>
<s> the board draws hurriedly together and forms a group <\s>
<s> tench in a frightened manner speaks into the hall <\s>
<s> underwood almost forces enid from the room wilder <\s>
<s> hurriedly what's to be said to them <\s>
<s> tench writes in his book wanklin <\s>
<s> very well then i ask the chairman to put it to the board <\s>
<s> with a great sigh slowly we have been made the subject of an attack <\s>
<s> looking round at wilder and scantlebury with ironical contempt i take it on my shoulders <\s>
<s> i am seventy six years old <\s>
<s> i have been chairman of this company since its inception two and thirty years ago <\s>
<s> i have seen it pass through good and evil report <\s>
<s> my connection with it began in the year that this young man was born <\s>
<s> edgar bows his head <\s>
<s> anthony gripping his chair goes on i have had do to with men for fifty years i've always stood up to them i have never been beaten yet <\s>
<s> i have fought the men of this company four times and four times i have beaten them <\s>
<s> it has been said that i am not the man i was <\s>
<s> he looks at wilder however that may be i am man enough to stand to my guns <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger <\s>
<s> the double doors are opened <\s>
<s> enid slips in followed by underwood who restrains her the men have been treated justly they have had fair wages we have always been ready to listen to complaints <\s>
<s> it has been said that times have changed if they have i have not changed with them <\s>
<s> it has been said that masters and men are equal <\s>
<s> there can only be one master in a house <\s>
<s> where two men meet the better man will rule <\s>
<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>

<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>

<s> that will be my look out and this is his <\s>
<s> i cannot separate as i would these men from their women and children <\s>

<s> it has been said that times have changed if they have i have not changed with them <\s>
<s> it has been said that masters and men are equal <\s>
<s> there can only be one master in a house <\s>
<s> where two men meet the better man will rule <\s>
<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture of dismissal shall i bring them in sir <\s>
<s> frost goes out anthony turns to face his son i come to the attack that has been made upon me <\s>
<s> edgar with a gesture of deprecation remains motionless with his head a little bowed a woman has died <\s>
<s> i am told that her blood is on my hands i am told that on my hands is the starvation and the suffering of other women and of children <\s>
<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>
<s> if i fall under his feet as fall i may i shall not complain <\s>
<s> that will be my look out and this is his <\s>
<s> i cannot separate as i would these men from their women and children <\s>
<s> a fair fight is a fair fight <\s>
<s> let them learn to think before they pick a quarrel <\s>
<s> in a low voice but is it a fair fight father <\s>
<s> look at them and look at us <\s>
<s> they've only this one weapon <\s>
<s> grimly and you're weak kneed enough to teach them how to use it <\s>
<s> it seems the fashion nowadays for men to take their enemy's side <\s>
<s> i have not learnt that art <\s>
<s> is it my fault that they quarrelled with their union too <\s>
<s> there is such a thing as mercy <\s>
<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>
<s> with suppressed passion you accuse me of injustice of what amounts to inhumanity of cruelty <\s>
<s> edgar makes a gesture of horror a general frightened movement wanklin <\s>
<s> in a grim voice these are the words of my own son <\s>
<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>
<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>

<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>
<s> with suppressed passion you accuse me of injustice of what amounts to inhumanity of cruelty <\s>
<s> edgar makes a gesture of horror a general frightened movement wanklin <\s>
<s> in a grim voice these are the words of my own son <\s>
<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>
<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>
<s> you have disgraced me gentlemen <\s>
<s> bring in the men <\s>
<s> he sits motionless staring before him <\s>
<s> the board draws hurriedly together and forms a group <\s>
<s> tench in a frightened manner speaks into the hall <\s>
<s> underwood almost forces enid from the room wilder <\s>
<s> hurriedly what's to be said to them <\s>
<s> tench writes in his book wanklin <\s>
<s> very well then i ask the chairman to put it to the board <\s>
<s> with a great sigh slowly we have been made the subject of an attack <\s>
<s> looking round at wilder and scantlebury with ironical contempt i take it on my shoulders <\s>
<s> i am seventy six years old <\s>
<s> i have been chairman of this company since its inception two and thirty years ago <\s>
<s> i have seen it pass through good and evil report <\s>
<s> my connection with it began in the year that this young man was born <\s>
<s> edgar bows his head <\s>
<s> anthony gripping his chair goes on i have had do to with men for fifty years i've always stood up to them i have never been beaten yet <\s>
<s> i have fought the men of this company four times and four times i have beaten them <\s>
<s> it has been said that i am not the man i was <\s>
<s> he looks at wilder however that may be i am man enough to stand to my guns <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger <\s>
<s> the double doors are opened <\s>
<s> enid slips in followed by underwood who restrains her the men have been treated justly they have had fair wages we have always been ready to listen to complaints <\s>
<s> it has been said that times have changed if they have i have not changed with them <\s>
<s> it has been said that masters and men are equal <\s>
<s> there can only be one master in a house <\s>
<s> where two men meet the better man will rule <\s>
<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>

<s> he looks at wilder however that may be i am man enough to stand to my guns <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger <\s>
<s> the double doors are opened <\s>
<s> enid slips in followed by underwood who restrains her the men have been treated justly they have had fair wages we have always been ready to listen to complaints <\s>
<s> it has been said that times have changed if they have i have not changed with them <\s>
<s> it has been said that masters and men are equal <\s>
<s> there can only be one master in a house <\s>
<s> where two men meet the better man will rule <\s>
<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture of dismissal shall i bring them in sir <\s>
<s> frost goes out anthony turns to face his son i come to the attack that has been made upon me <\s>
<s> edgar with a gesture of deprecation remains motionless with his head a little bowed a woman has died <\s>
<s> i am told that her blood is on my hands i am told that on my hands is the starvation and the suffering of other women and of children <\s>
<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>
<s> if i fall under his feet as fall i may i shall not complain <\s>
<s> that will be my look out and this is his <\s>
<s> i cannot separate as i would these men from their women and children <\s>
<s> a fair fight is a fair fight <\s>
<s> let them learn to think before they pick a quarrel <\s>
<s> in a low voice but is it a fair fight father <\s>
<s> look at them and look at us <\s>
<s> they've only this one weapon <\s>
<s> grimly and you're weak kneed enough to teach them how to use it <\s>
<s> it seems the fashion nowadays for men to take their enemy's side <\s>
<s> i have not learnt that art <\s>
<s> is it my fault that they quarrelled with their union too <\s>
<s> there is such a thing as mercy <\s>
<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>
<s> with suppressed passion you accuse me of injustice of what amounts to inhumanity of cruelty <\s>
<s> edgar makes a gesture of horror a general frightened movement wanklin <\s>
<s> in a grim voice these are the words of my own son <\s>
<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>
<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>

<s> grimly and you're weak kneed enough to teach them how to use it <\s>
<s> it seems the fashion nowadays for men to take their enemy's side <\s>
<s> i have not learnt that art <\s>
<s> is it my fault that they quarrelled with their union too <\s>
<s> there is such a thing as mercy <\s>
<s> and justice comes before it <\s>
<s> what seems just to one man sir is injustice to another <\s>
<s> with suppressed passion you accuse me of injustice of what amounts to inhumanity of cruelty <\s>
<s> edgar makes a gesture of horror a general frightened movement wanklin <\s>
<s> in a grim voice these are the words of my own son <\s>
<s> they are the words of a generation that i don't understand the words of a soft breed <\s>
<s> with a violent effort anthony recovers his control edgar <\s>
<s> quietly i said it of myself too father <\s>
<s> a long look is exchanged between them and anthony puts out his hand with a gesture as if to sweep the personalities away then places it against his brow swaying as though from giddiness <\s>
<s> there is a movement towards him <\s>
<s> he moves them back anthony <\s>
<s> before i put this amendment to the board i have one more word to say <\s>
<s> he looks from face to face if it is carried it means that we shall fail in what we set ourselves to do <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe to all capital <\s>
<s> it means that we shall fail in the duty that we owe ourselves <\s>
<s> it means that we shall be open to constant attack to which we as constantly shall have to yield <\s>
<s> be under no misapprehension run this time and you will never make a stand again <\s>
<s> you will have to fly like curs before the whips of your own men <\s>
<s> if that is the lot you wish for you will vote for this amendment <\s>
<s> he looks again from face to face finally resting his gaze on edgar all sit with their eyes on the ground <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture and tench hands him the book <\s>
<s> he reads moved by mr <\s>
<s> wilder and seconded by mr <\s>
<s> wanklin that the men's demands be placed at once in the hands of mr <\s>
<s> simon harness for settlement on the lines indicated by him this morning with sudden vigour those in favour signify the same in the usual way <\s>
<s> for a minute no one moves then hastily just as anthony is about to speak wilder's hand and wanklin's are held up then scantlebury's and last edgar's who does not lift his head anthony lifts his own hand in a clear voice the amendment is carried <\s>
<s> i resign my position on this board <\s>
<s> enid gasps and there is dead silence <\s>
<s> anthony sits motionless his head slowly drooping suddenly he heaves as though the whole of his life had risen up within him contrary <\s>
<s> you have disgraced me gentlemen <\s>
<s> bring in the men <\s>
<s> he sits motionless staring before him <\s>
<s> the board draws hurriedly together and forms a group <\s>
<s> tench in a frightened manner speaks into the hall <\s>
<s> underwood almost forces enid from the room wilder <\s>
<s> hurriedly what's to be said to them <\s>
<s> tench writes in his book wanklin <\s>
<s> very well then i ask the chairman to put it to the board <\s>
<s> with a great sigh slowly we have been made the subject of an attack <\s>
<s> looking round at wilder and scantlebury with ironical contempt i take it on my shoulders <\s>
<s> i am seventy six years old <\s>
<s> i have been chairman of this company since its inception two and thirty years ago <\s>
<s> i have seen it pass through good and evil report <\s>
<s> my connection with it began in the year that this young man was born <\s>
<s> edgar bows his head <\s>
<s> anthony gripping his chair goes on i have had do to with men for fifty years i've always stood up to them i have never been beaten yet <\s>
<s> i have fought the men of this company four times and four times i have beaten them <\s>
<s> it has been said that i am not the man i was <\s>
<s> he looks at wilder however that may be i am man enough to stand to my guns <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger <\s>
<s> the double doors are opened <\s>
<s> enid slips in followed by underwood who restrains her the men have been treated justly they have had fair wages we have always been ready to listen to complaints <\s>
<s> it has been said that times have changed if they have i have not changed with them <\s>
<s> it has been said that masters and men are equal <\s>
<s> there can only be one master in a house <\s>
<s> where two men meet the better man will rule <\s>
<s> it has been said that capital and labour have the same interests <\s>
<s> their interests are as wide asunder as the poles <\s>
<s> it has been said that the board is only part of a machine <\s>
<s> we are the machine its brains and sinews it is for us to lead and to determine what is to be done and to do it without fear or favour <\s>
<s> fear of the men <\s>
<s> fear of the shareholders <\s>
<s> fear of our own shadows <\s>
<s> before i am like that i hope to die <\s>
<s> he pauses and meeting his son's eyes goes on there is only one way of treating men with the iron hand <\s>
<s> this half and half business the half and half manners of this generation has brought all this upon us <\s>
<s> sentiment and softness and what this young man no doubt would call his social policy <\s>
<s> you can't eat cake and have it <\s>
<s> this middle class sentiment or socialism or whatever it may be is rotten <\s>
<s> masters are masters men are men <\s>
<s> yield one demand and they will make it six <\s>
<s> they are he smiles grimly like oliver twist asking for more <\s>
<s> if i were in their place i should be the same <\s>
<s> but i am not in their place <\s>
<s> mark my words one fine morning when you have given way here and given way there you will find you have parted with the ground beneath your feet and are deep in the bog of bankruptcy and with you floundering in that bog will be the very men you have given way to <\s>
<s> i have been accused of being a domineering tyrant thinking only of my pride i am thinking of the future of this country threatened with the black waters of confusion threatened with mob government threatened with what i cannot see <\s>
<s> if by any conduct of mine i help to bring this on us i shall be ashamed to look my fellows in the face <\s>
<s> anthony stares before him at what he cannot see and there is perfect stillness <\s>
<s> frost comes in from the hall and all but anthony look round at him uneasily frost <\s>
<s> to his master the men are here sir <\s>
<s> anthony makes a gesture of dismissal shall i bring them in sir <\s>
<s> frost goes out anthony turns to face his son i come to the attack that has been made upon me <\s>
<s> edgar with a gesture of deprecation remains motionless with his head a little bowed a woman has died <\s>
<s> i am told that her blood is on my hands i am told that on my hands is the starvation and the suffering of other women and of children <\s>
<s> i said on our hands sir <\s>
<s> it is the same <\s>
<s> his voice grows stronger and stronger his feeling is more and more made manifest i am not aware that if my adversary suffer in a fair fight not sought by me it is my fault <\s>
